#### 5.4.4 技术栈速查表

| 类别 | 技术 | 用途 | 面试高频问题 |
|------|------|------|-------------|
| **框架** | Next.js 14/16 | SSR/SSG | App Router vs Pages Router |
| | React 18/19 | UI 库 | Fiber 架构、Hooks 原理 |
| | NestJS | 后端框架 | 依赖注入、模块系统 |
| **状态管理** | Zustand | 轻量级状态 | 与 Redux 区别、persist |
| | Immer | 不可变更新 | 原理、使用场景 |
| **编辑器** | TipTap | 富文本编辑 | ProseMirror 架构 |
| | Monaco Editor | 代码编辑 | 懒加载、性能优化 |
| **协作** | Yjs | CRDT 协作 | 冲突解决、与 OT 区别 |
| | Socket.io | 实时通信 | 房间管理、心跳 |
| **3D** | Three.js | 3D 渲染 | 渲染流程、几何体 |
| | R3F | React+Three | 组件化开发 | useFrame、Hooks |
| **UI** | Ant Design | 组件库 | 主题定制、Tree Shaking |
| | Tailwind CSS | 原子化 CSS | 原理、 purgecss |
| | Framer Motion | 动画 | AnimatePresence |
| **构建** | Webpack | 模块打包 | 原理、loader |
| | Vite | 开发服务器 | HMR、热更新 |
| | Turbopack | 构建工具 | 与 Webpack 对比 |
| **视频** | LiveKit | WebRTC | SFU vs MCU |
| | WebRTC | 实时通信 | 媒体轨道、ICE |

#### 5.4.5 项目技术选择理由

```typescript
// 1. 为什么选择 Zustand 而非 Redux？
/*
Zustand 优势：
- 极简 API：create((set) => ({ count: 0 }))
- 无 Provider 嵌套：store 可以直接 import
- 灵活更新：set(state => ({ count: state.count + 1 }))
- 轻量级：体积仅 1KB
- TypeScript 支持好

适用场景：
- 中小型项目
- 需要简单状态管理
- 对性能有要求

不适用：
- 超大型项目（需要严格架构）
- 团队对 Redux 熟悉
*/

// 2. 为什么选择 TipTap 而非 Slate？
/*
TipTap 优势：
- 基于 ProseMirror（生产级）
- Yjs 原生支持协作
- 丰富的扩展生态
- 文档完善

Slate 优势：
- 更灵活的自定义
- 学习曲线陡峭但可定制性强

选择 TipTap：协作优先
选择 Slate：高度自定义需求
*/

// 3. 为什么选择 Yjs 而非 Automerge？
/*
Yjs 优势：
- 性能更好
- WebSocket 同步方案成熟
- 丰富的生态系统 (y-websocket, y-indexeddb)
- ProseMirror/Monaco 原生支持

Automerge 优势：
- API 更简洁
- 文档更好

性能对比：Yjs > Automerge
生态丰富：Yjs > Automerge
*/

// 4. 为什么选择 React Three Fiber？
/*
R3F 优势：
- React 开发范式
- 组件化思维
- 生态丰富 (@react-three/drei)
- 与 React DevTools 集成

Three.js 优势：
- 更底层控制
- 无 React 依赖

选择 R3F：熟悉 React
选择 Three.js：熟悉 3D 开发
*/
```

---

#### 5.4.6 WebEnv-OS 桌面操作系统完整实现

以下提供 WebEnv-OS 项目的完整实现代码，包括窗口管理系统、拖拽组件、任务栏、文件资源管理器等核心模块。

##### 窗口管理系统

```typescript
// 窗口管理核心实现

// 窗口状态接口
interface WindowState {
  id: string;
  title: string;
  icon?: string;
  content: React.ReactNode;
  position: { x: number; y: number };
  size: { width: number; height: number };
  zIndex: number;
  isMinimized: boolean;
  isMaximized: boolean;
  isFullscreen: boolean;
  isFocused: boolean;
  resizable: boolean;
  draggable: boolean;
  closeable: boolean;
  minSize?: { width: number; height: number };
  maxSize?: { width: number; height: number };
}

// 窗口管理器 Hook
import { create } from 'zustand';

interface WindowManager {
  windows: WindowState[];
  activeWindowId: string | null;

  // 窗口操作
  openWindow: (window: Omit<WindowState, 'zIndex' | 'isFocused'>) => void;
  closeWindow: (id: string) => void;
  minimizeWindow: (id: string) => void;
  maximizeWindow: (id: string) => void;
  restoreWindow: (id: string) => void;

  // 窗口位置和大小
  moveWindow: (id: string, position: { x: number; y: number }) => void;
  resizeWindow: (id: string, size: { width: number; height: number }) => void;

  // 焦点管理
  focusWindow: (id: string) => void;

  // 窗口排序
  bringToFront: (id: string) => void;
  sendToBack: (id: string) => void;
}

const useWindowManager = create<WindowManager>((set, get) => ({
  windows: [],
  activeWindowId: null,

  openWindow: (windowConfig) => {
    const { windows } = get();
    const maxZIndex = Math.max(0, ...windows.map(w => w.zIndex));

    const newWindow: WindowState = {
      ...windowConfig,
      id: windowConfig.id || `window-${Date.now()}`,
      zIndex: maxZIndex + 1,
      isFocused: true,
    };

    set({
      windows: [...windows, newWindow],
      activeWindowId: newWindow.id,
    });
  },

  closeWindow: (id) => {
    const { windows, activeWindowId } = get();
    const newWindows = windows.filter(w => w.id !== id);

    // 如果关闭的是活动窗口，激活另一个
    let newActiveId = activeWindowId;
    if (activeWindowId === id) {
      const closedIndex = windows.findIndex(w => w.id === id);
      const nextWindow = newWindows[closedIndex] || newWindows[newWindows.length - 1];
      newActiveId = nextWindow?.id || null;
    }

    set({
      windows: newWindows,
      activeWindowId: newActiveId,
    });
  },

  minimizeWindow: (id) => {
    set(state => ({
      windows: state.windows.map(w =>
        w.id === id ? { ...w, isMinimized: true, isFocused: false } : w
      ),
    }));
  },

  maximizeWindow: (id) => {
    set(state => ({
      windows: state.windows.map(w =>
        w.id === id ? { ...w, isMaximized: true, isFocused: true } : w
      ),
    }));
  },

  restoreWindow: (id) => {
    set(state => ({
      windows: state.windows.map(w =>
        w.id === id ? { ...w, isMinimized: false, isMaximized: false, isFocused: true } : w
      ),
    }));
  },

  moveWindow: (id, position) => {
    set(state => ({
      windows: state.windows.map(w =>
        w.id === id ? { ...w, position } : w
      ),
    }));
  },

  resizeWindow: (id, size) => {
    set(state => ({
      windows: state.windows.map(w =>
        w.id === id ? { ...w, size } : w
      ),
    }));
  },

  focusWindow: (id) => {
    const { windows } = get();
    const maxZIndex = Math.max(0, ...windows.map(w => w.zIndex));

    set(state => ({
      windows: state.windows.map(w => ({
        ...w,
        isFocused: w.id === id,
        zIndex: w.id === id ? maxZIndex + 1 : w.zIndex,
      })),
      activeWindowId: id,
    }));
  },

  bringToFront: (id) => {
    const { windows } = get();
    const maxZIndex = Math.max(0, ...windows.map(w => w.zIndex));

    set(state => ({
      windows: state.windows.map(w =>
        w.id === id ? { ...w, zIndex: maxZIndex + 1, isFocused: true } : w
      ),
    }));
  },

  sendToBack: (id) => {
    set(state => ({
      windows: state.windows.map(w =>
        w.id === id ? { ...w, zIndex: 0 } : { ...w, zIndex: w.zIndex + 1 }
      ),
    }));
  },
}));
```

**面试考察点：**
- Zustand 状态管理设计
- 窗口 z-index 层级管理
- 窗口状态机设计
- 焦点管理策略

##### 窗口拖拽实现

```typescript
// 窗口拖拽组件实现
import React, { useRef, useState, useCallback } from 'react';
import { useWindowManager } from './useWindowManager';

interface DraggableWindowProps {
  window: WindowState;
  children: React.ReactNode;
}

export const DraggableWindow: React.FC<DraggableWindowProps> = ({
  window,
  children,
}) => {
  const { moveWindow, focusWindow, resizeWindow } = useWindowManager();
  const windowRef = useRef<HTMLDivElement>(null);

  const [isDragging, setIsDragging] = useState(false);
  const [isResizing, setIsResizing] = useState(false);
  const [resizeDirection, setResizeDirection] = useState<string>('');

  const dragStartPos = useRef({ x: 0, y: 0 });
  const windowStartPos = useRef({ x: 0, y: 0 });
  const windowStartSize = useRef({ width: 0, height: 0 });

  // 开始拖拽
  const handleDragStart = useCallback((e: React.MouseEvent) => {
    if (window.isMaximized || window.isMinimized) return;

    e.preventDefault();
    setIsDragging(true);
    focusWindow(window.id);

    dragStartPos.current = { x: e.clientX, y: e.clientY };
    windowStartPos.current = { ...window.position };

    const handleMouseMove = (e: MouseEvent) => {
      const deltaX = e.clientX - dragStartPos.current.x;
      const deltaY = e.clientY - dragStartPos.current.y;

      const newX = Math.max(0, windowStartPos.current.x + deltaX);
      const newY = Math.max(0, windowStartPos.current.y + deltaY);

      moveWindow(window.id, { x: newX, y: newY });
    };

    const handleMouseUp = () => {
      setIsDragging(false);
      document.removeEventListener('mousemove', handleMouseMove);
      document.removeEventListener('mouseup', handleMouseUp);
    };

    document.addEventListener('mousemove', handleMouseMove);
    document.addEventListener('mouseup', handleMouseUp);
  }, [window, focusWindow, moveWindow]);

  // 开始调整大小
  const handleResizeStart = useCallback((e: React.MouseEvent, direction: string) => {
    e.preventDefault();
    e.stopPropagation();

    setIsResizing(true);
    setResizeDirection(direction);
    focusWindow(window.id);

    dragStartPos.current = { x: e.clientX, y: e.clientY };
    windowStartPos.current = { ...window.position };
    windowStartSize.current = { ...window.size };

    const handleMouseMove = (e: MouseEvent) => {
      const deltaX = e.clientX - dragStartPos.current.x;
      const deltaY = e.clientY - dragStartPos.current.y;

      let newWidth = windowStartSize.current.width;
      let newHeight = windowStartSize.current.height;
      let newX = windowStartPos.current.x;
      let newY = windowStartPos.current.y;

      // 根据方向调整大小
      if (direction.includes('e')) {
        newWidth = Math.max(200, windowStartSize.current.width + deltaX);
      }
      if (direction.includes('s')) {
        newHeight = Math.max(150, windowStartSize.current.height + deltaY);
      }
      if (direction.includes('w')) {
        newWidth = Math.max(200, windowStartSize.current.width - deltaX);
        newX = windowStartPos.current.x + deltaX;
      }
      if (direction.includes('n')) {
        newHeight = Math.max(150, windowStartSize.current.height - deltaY);
        newY = windowStartPos.current.y + deltaY;
      }

      resizeWindow(window.id, { width: newWidth, height: newHeight });
      if (direction.includes('w') || direction.includes('n')) {
        moveWindow(window.id, { x: newX, y: newY });
      }
    };

    const handleMouseUp = () => {
      setIsResizing(false);
      setResizeDirection('');
      document.removeEventListener('mousemove', handleMouseMove);
      document.removeEventListener('mouseup', handleMouseUp);
    };

    document.addEventListener('mousemove', handleMouseMove);
    document.addEventListener('mouseup', handleMouseUp);
  }, [window, focusWindow, resizeWindow, moveWindow]);

  return (
    <div
      ref={windowRef}
      className={`window ${isDragging ? 'dragging' : ''} ${isResizing ? 'resizing' : ''}`}
      style={{
        position: 'absolute',
        left: window.position.x,
        top: window.position.y,
        width: window.size.width,
        height: window.size.height,
        zIndex: window.zIndex,
        display: window.isMinimized ? 'none' : 'flex',
        flexDirection: 'column',
      }}
    >
      {/* 标题栏 */}
      <div
        className="window-titlebar flex items-center justify-between px-2 py-1 bg-gray-800 text-white cursor-move"
        onMouseDown={handleDragStart}
      >
        <div className="flex items-center gap-2">
          {window.icon && <span className="text-lg">{window.icon}</span>}
          <span className="text-sm">{window.title}</span>
        </div>
        <WindowControls windowId={window.id} />
      </div>

      {/* 窗口内容 */}
      <div className="window-content flex-1 overflow-auto">
        {children}
      </div>

      {/* 调整大小手柄 */}
      {!window.isMaximized && (
        <>
          <div className="resize-handle resize-e" onMouseDown={(e) => handleResizeStart(e, 'e')} />
          <div className="resize-handle resize-s" onMouseDown={(e) => handleResizeStart(e, 's')} />
          <div className="resize-handle resize-w" onMouseDown={(e) => handleResizeStart(e, 'w')} />
          <div className="resize-handle resize-n" onMouseDown={(e) => handleResizeStart(e, 'n')} />
          <div className="resize-handle resize-se" onMouseDown={(e) => handleResizeStart(e, 'se')} />
          <div className="resize-handle resize-sw" onMouseDown={(e) => handleResizeStart(e, 'sw')} />
          <div className="resize-handle resize-ne" onMouseDown={(e) => handleResizeStart(e, 'ne')} />
          <div className="resize-handle resize-nw" onMouseDown={(e) => handleResizeStart(e, 'nw')} />
        </>
      )}
    </div>
  );
};
```

**面试考察点：**
- 鼠标事件处理
- 坐标计算与边界检测
- DOM 事件委托
- 性能优化（事件绑定位置）

##### 任务栏实现

```typescript
// 任务栏组件实现
import React, { useState, useRef } from 'react';
import { useWindowManager } from './useWindowManager';

export const Taskbar: React.FC = () => {
  const { windows, activeWindowId, focusWindow, minimizeWindow, restoreWindow } = useWindowManager();
  const [startMenuOpen, setStartMenuOpen] = useState(false);
  const taskbarRef = useRef<HTMLDivElement>(null);

  // 开始菜单应用列表
  const startMenuApps = [
    { id: 'explorer', name: '文件资源管理器', icon: '📁' },
    { id: 'browser', name: '浏览器', icon: '🌐' },
    { id: 'vscode', name: 'VS Code', icon: '💻' },
    { id: 'terminal', name: '终端', icon: '⬛' },
    { id: 'settings', name: '设置', icon: '⚙️' },
  ];

  // 打开应用
  const openApp = (appId: string) => {
    // 触发应用打开事件
    console.log('Opening app:', appId);
    setStartMenuOpen(false);
  };

  // 点击任务栏窗口图标
  const handleTaskbarItemClick = (windowId: string) => {
    const win = windows.find(w => w.id === windowId);
    if (!win) return;

    if (win.isMinimized) {
      restoreWindow(windowId);
    } else if (win.isFocused) {
      minimizeWindow(windowId);
    } else {
      focusWindow(windowId);
    }
  };

  return (
    <div
      ref={taskbarRef}
      className="taskbar fixed bottom-0 left-0 right-0 h-12 bg-gray-900 flex items-center px-2 z-[9999]"
    >
      {/* 开始按钮 */}
      <button
        className={`start-button w-10 h-10 flex items-center justify-center text-2xl hover:bg-gray-700 rounded ${startMenuOpen ? 'bg-gray-700' : ''}`}
        onClick={() => setStartMenuOpen(!startMenuOpen)}
      >
        🪟
      </button>

      {/* 开始菜单 */}
      {startMenuOpen && (
        <>
          <div
            className="fixed inset-0"
            onClick={() => setStartMenuOpen(false)}
          />
          <div className="start-menu absolute bottom-14 left-2 w-64 bg-gray-800 rounded-lg shadow-xl overflow-hidden">
            <div className="pinned-apps grid grid-cols-4 gap-2 p-2">
              {startMenuApps.map(app => (
                <button
                  key={app.id}
                  className="app-button flex flex-col items-center justify-center p-2 rounded hover:bg-gray-700"
                  onClick={() => openApp(app.id)}
                >
                  <span className="text-2xl">{app.icon}</span>
                  <span className="text-xs mt-1">{app.name}</span>
                </button>
              ))}
            </div>
          </div>
        </>
      )}

      {/* 任务栏窗口列表 */}
      <div className="taskbar-items flex-1 flex items-center gap-1 ml-2 overflow-x-auto">
        {windows.map(win => (
          <button
            key={win.id}
            className={`taskbar-item flex items-center gap-2 px-3 h-9 rounded transition-colors ${
              win.id === activeWindowId && !win.isMinimized
                ? 'bg-gray-700'
                : 'hover:bg-gray-700'
            }`}
            onClick={() => handleTaskbarItemClick(win.id)}
          >
            {win.icon && <span>{win.icon}</span>}
            <span className="text-sm truncate max-w-[100px]">{win.title}</span>
          </button>
        ))}
      </div>

      {/* 系统托盘 */}
      <div className="system-tray flex items-center gap-2 px-2">
        <button className="tray-icon">🔔</button>
        <button className="tray-icon">⚙️</button>
        <span className="text-sm">{new Date().toLocaleTimeString()}</span>
      </div>
    </div>
  );
};
```

**面试考察点：**
- 组件状态管理
- 用户交互设计
- 响应式布局
- 事件冒泡处理

##### 文件资源管理器实现（树形结构）

```typescript
// 文件资源管理器 - 树形结构实现
import React, { useState, useCallback } from 'react';
import { create } from 'zustand';

// 文件/文件夹类型定义
interface FileItem {
  id: string;
  name: string;
  type: 'file' | 'folder';
  path: string;
  children?: FileItem[];
  expanded?: boolean;
  size?: number;
  modifiedTime?: Date;
}

// 文件管理器状态
interface FileManagerState {
  files: FileItem[];
  selectedFile: string | null;
  expandedFolders: Set<string>;

  // 操作方法
  toggleFolder: (id: string) => void;
  selectFile: (id: string) => void;
  createFile: (parentId: string, name: string, type: 'file' | 'folder') => void;
  deleteFile: (id: string) => void;
  renameFile: (id: string, newName: string) => void;
  moveFile: (id: string, newParentId: string) => void;
}

// 初始化文件数据
const initialFiles: FileItem[] = [
  {
    id: 'root',
    name: '我的电脑',
    type: 'folder',
    path: '/',
    expanded: true,
    children: [
      {
        id: 'desktop',
        name: '桌面',
        type: 'folder',
        path: '/desktop',
        children: [
          { id: 'file1', name: '新建文档.txt', type: 'file', path: '/desktop/file1.txt', size: 1024 },
          { id: 'file2', name: '图片.png', type: 'file', path: '/desktop/image.png', size: 2048000 },
        ],
      },
      {
        id: 'documents',
        name: '文档',
        type: 'folder',
        path: '/documents',
        children: [
          { id: 'folder1', name: '项目', type: 'folder', path: '/documents/project' },
          { id: 'file3', name: '笔记.md', type: 'file', path: '/documents/notes.md', size: 4096 },
        ],
      },
      {
        id: 'downloads',
        name: '下载',
        type: 'folder',
        path: '/downloads',
        children: [],
      },
    ],
  },
];

// 创建文件管理器 Store
const useFileManager = create<FileManagerState>((set, get) => ({
  files: initialFiles,
  selectedFile: null,
  expandedFolders: new Set(['root']),

  toggleFolder: (id) => {
    set(state => {
      const newExpanded = new Set(state.expandedFolders);
      if (newExpanded.has(id)) {
        newExpanded.delete(id);
      } else {
        newExpanded.add(id);
      }
      return { expandedFolders: newExpanded };
    });
  },

  selectFile: (id) => {
    set({ selectedFile: id });
  },

  createFile: (parentId, name, type) => {
    const newFile: FileItem = {
      id: `file-${Date.now()}`,
      name,
      type,
      path: `/${parentId}/${name}`,
      children: type === 'folder' ? [] : undefined,
    };

    // 递归查找并添加文件
    const addFile = (files: FileItem[]): FileItem[] => {
      return files.map(file => {
        if (file.id === parentId && file.type === 'folder') {
          return {
            ...file,
            children: [...(file.children || []), newFile],
          };
        }
        if (file.children) {
          return { ...file, children: addFile(file.children) };
        }
        return file;
      });
    };

    set(state => ({ files: addFile(state.files) }));
  },

  deleteFile: (id) => {
    const deleteFileRecursive = (files: FileItem[]): FileItem[] => {
      return files
        .filter(file => file.id !== id)
        .map(file => ({
          ...file,
          children: file.children ? deleteFileRecursive(file.children) : undefined,
        }));
    };

    set(state => ({ files: deleteFileRecursive(state.files) }));
  },

  renameFile: (id, newName) => {
    const rename = (files: FileItem[]): FileItem[] => {
      return files.map(file => {
        if (file.id === id) {
          return { ...file, name: newName };
        }
        if (file.children) {
          return { ...file, children: rename(file.children) };
        }
        return file;
      });
    };

    set(state => ({ files: rename(state.files) }));
  },

  moveFile: (id, newParentId) => {
    // 移动文件逻辑
    console.log('Moving file:', id, 'to', newParentId);
  },
}));

// 文件树组件
export const FileTree: React.FC = () => {
  const { files, selectedFile, expandedFolders, toggleFolder, selectFile } = useFileManager();

  const renderFile = (file: FileItem, depth: number = 0): React.ReactNode => {
    const isFolder = file.type === 'folder';
    const isExpanded = expandedFolders.has(file.id);
    const isSelected = selectedFile === file.id;

    return (
      <div key={file.id}>
        <div
          className={`file-item flex items-center gap-2 py-1 px-2 cursor-pointer hover:bg-gray-700 ${
            isSelected ? 'bg-blue-600' : ''
          }`}
          style={{ paddingLeft: `${depth * 16 + 8}px` }}
          onClick={() => {
            selectFile(file.id);
            if (isFolder) {
              toggleFolder(file.id);
            }
          }}
        >
          {/* 展开/折叠图标 */}
          {isFolder ? (
            <span className="text-gray-400">
              {isExpanded ? '▼' : '▶'}
            </span>
          ) : (
            <span className="w-4" />
          )}

          {/* 文件/文件夹图标 */}
          <span className="text-lg">
            {isFolder ? (isExpanded ? '📂' : '📁') : getFileIcon(file.name)}
          </span>

          {/* 文件名 */}
          <span className="text-sm truncate">{file.name}</span>

          {/* 文件大小 */}
          {!isFolder && file.size && (
            <span className="text-xs text-gray-500 ml-auto">
              {formatFileSize(file.size)}
            </span>
          )}
        </div>

        {/* 递归渲染子文件 */}
        {isFolder && isExpanded && file.children && (
          <div className="children">
            {file.children.map(child => renderFile(child, depth + 1))}
          </div>
        )}
      </div>
    );
  };

  return (
    <div className="file-tree">
      {files.map(file => renderFile(file))}
    </div>
  );
};

// 工具函数
function getFileIcon(filename: string): string {
  const ext = filename.split('.').pop()?.toLowerCase();
  const icons: Record<string, string> = {
    txt: '📄',
    md: '📝',
    js: '📜',
    ts: '📜',
    jsx: '⚛️',
    tsx: '⚛️',
    json: '📋',
    png: '🖼️',
    jpg: '🖼️',
    jpeg: '🖼️',
    gif: '🖼️',
    mp3: '🎵',
    mp4: '🎬',
    zip: '📦',
    rar: '📦',
    pdf: '📕',
    doc: '📘',
    docx: '📘',
    xls: '📗',
    xlsx: '📗',
  };
  return icons[ext || ''] || '📄';
}

function formatFileSize(bytes: number): string {
  if (bytes < 1024) return bytes + ' B';
  if (bytes < 1024 * 1024) return (bytes / 1024).toFixed(1) + ' KB';
  return (bytes / (1024 * 1024)).toFixed(1) + ' MB';
}
```

**面试考察点：**
- 树形数据结构设计
- 递归组件渲染
- Zustand 状态管理
- 文件操作 CRUD

##### 终端模拟器实现（xterm.js 集成）

```typescript
// 终端模拟器组件 - xterm.js 集成
import React, { useEffect, useRef, useState } from 'react';
import { Terminal } from 'xterm';
import { FitAddon } from 'xterm-addon-fit';
import { WebLinksAddon } from 'xterm-addon-web-links';
import 'xterm/css/xterm.css';

interface TerminalProps {
  onData?: (data: string) => void;
  onResize?: (cols: number, rows: number) => void;
}

export const VirtualTerminal: React.FC<TerminalProps> = ({ onData, onResize }) => {
  const terminalRef = useRef<HTMLDivElement>(null);
  const terminalInstance = useRef<Terminal | null>(null);
  const fitAddon = useRef<FitAddon | null>(null);
  const [isReady, setIsReady] = useState(false);

  useEffect(() => {
    if (!terminalRef.current) return;

    // 创建终端实例
    const terminal = new Terminal({
      cursorBlink: true,
      fontSize: 14,
      fontFamily: 'Menlo, Monaco, "Courier New", monospace',
      theme: {
        background: '#1e1e1e',
        foreground: '#d4d4d4',
        cursor: '#ffffff',
        selection: '#264f78',
        black: '#000000',
        red: '#cd3131',
        green: '#0dbc79',
        yellow: '#e5e510',
        blue: '#2472c8',
        magenta: '#bc3fbc',
        cyan: '#11a8cd',
        white: '#e5e5e5',
        brightBlack: '#666666',
        brightRed: '#f14c4c',
        brightGreen: '#23d18b',
        brightYellow: '#f5f543',
        brightBlue: '#3b8eea',
        brightMagenta: '#d670d6',
        brightCyan: '#29b8db',
        brightWhite: '#ffffff',
      },
      allowTransparency: true,
      scrollback: 1000,
    });

    // 创建插件
    const fit = new FitAddon();
    const webLinks = new WebLinksAddon();

    // 加载插件
    terminal.loadAddon(fit);
    terminal.loadAddon(webLinks);

    // 打开终端
    terminal.open(terminalRef.current);
    fit.fit();

    // 设置终端实例
    terminalInstance.current = terminal;
    fitAddon.current = fit;
    setIsReady(true);

    // 监听数据输入
    terminal.onData((data) => {
      onData?.(data);
      // 模拟简单的 shell 响应
      handleTerminalInput(data, terminal);
    });

    // 监听终端尺寸变化
    terminal.onResize(({ cols, rows }) => {
      onResize?.(cols, rows);
    });

    // 初始欢迎信息
    terminal.writeln('\x1b[1;34m WebEnv-OS Terminal \x1b[0m');
    terminal.writeln('Type "help" for available commands.');
    terminal.write('\r\n$ ');

    // 处理终端输入
    const handleTerminalInput = (data: string, term: Terminal) => {
      const code = data.charCodeAt(0);

      if (code === 13) { // Enter
        term.writeln('');
        // 处理命令
        processCommand(term);
      } else if (code === 127) { // Backspace
        if (term._core.buffer.x > 2) {
          term.write('\b \b');
        }
      } else if (code < 32) {
        // 控制字符
      } else {
        term.write(data);
      }
    };

    // 命令处理
    const processCommand = (term: Terminal) => {
      const buffer = term._core.buffer;
      // 简化实现，实际需要更复杂的命令解析
      term.write('$ ');
    };

    // 窗口大小调整时自适应
    const handleResize = () => {
      fit.fit();
    };

    window.addEventListener('resize', handleResize);

    // 清理
    return () => {
      window.removeEventListener('resize', handleResize);
      terminal.dispose();
    };
  }, []);

  // 暴露写方法给父组件
  useEffect(() => {
    if (terminalInstance.current && isReady) {
      // 可以通过 ref 或 context 暴露方法
    }
  }, [isReady]);

  return (
    <div className="terminal-container bg-[#1e1e1e] p-2 rounded">
      <div ref={terminalRef} className="terminal" />
    </div>
  );
};

// 使用示例
export const TerminalApp: React.FC = () => {
  const handleData = (data: string) => {
    console.log('Terminal input:', data);
  };

  const handleResize = (cols: number, rows: number) => {
    console.log('Terminal resized:', cols, rows);
  };

  return (
    <div className="h-full w-full">
      <VirtualTerminal onData={handleData} onResize={handleResize} />
    </div>
  );
};
```

**面试考察点：**
- xterm.js 配置与定制
- 终端模拟器原理
- 事件处理与数据流
- 响应式适配

##### 桌面图标网格布局

```typescript
// 桌面图标网格布局实现
import React, { useState, useCallback } from 'react';
import { create } from 'zustand';

interface DesktopIcon {
  id: string;
  name: string;
  icon: string;
  position: { x: number; y: number };
  onClick: () => void;
}

interface DesktopState {
  icons: DesktopIcon[];
  selectedIcon: string | null;
  isDragging: boolean;

  // 操作
  selectIcon: (id: string) => void;
  moveIcon: (id: string, position: { x: number; y: number }) => void;
  setDragging: (isDragging: boolean) => void;
}

const GRID_SIZE = 100; // 网格大小
const ICON_SIZE = 80;  // 图标大小

const useDesktopStore = create<DesktopState>((set) => ({
  icons: [
    { id: '1', name: '回收站', icon: '🗑️', position: { x: 0, y: 0 }, onClick: () => {} },
    { id: '2', name: '我的电脑', icon: '💻', position: { x: 1, y: 0 }, onClick: () => {} },
    { id: '3', name: '浏览器', icon: '🌐', position: { x: 2, y: 0 }, onClick: () => {} },
    { id: '4', name: '文档', icon: '📁', position: { x: 0, y: 1 }, onClick: () => {} },
    { id: '5', name: '设置', icon: '⚙️', position: { x: 1, y: 1 }, onClick: () => {} },
  ],
  selectedIcon: null,
  isDragging: false,

  selectIcon: (id) => set({ selectedIcon: id }),

  moveIcon: (id, position) => {
    // 吸附到网格
    const snappedX = Math.round(position.x / GRID_SIZE) * GRID_SIZE;
    const snappedY = Math.round(position.y / GRID_SIZE) * GRID_SIZE;

    set(state => ({
      icons: state.icons.map(icon =>
        icon.id === id ? { ...icon, position: { x: snappedX, y: snappedY } } : icon
      ),
    }));
  },

  setDragging: (isDragging) => set({ isDragging }),
}));

export const Desktop: React.FC = () => {
  const { icons, selectedIcon, selectIcon, moveIcon, setDragging } = useDesktopStore();
  const [draggingId, setDraggingId] = useState<string | null>(null);
  const dragStartPos = useRef({ x: 0, y: 0 });
  const iconStartPos = useRef({ x: 0, y: 0 });

  const handleIconMouseDown = (e: React.MouseEvent, icon: DesktopIcon) => {
    e.preventDefault();
    setDraggingId(icon.id);
    setDragging(true);
    selectIcon(icon.id);

    dragStartPos.current = { x: e.clientX, y: e.clientY };
    iconStartPos.current = { ...icon.position };

    const handleMouseMove = (e: MouseEvent) => {
      const deltaX = e.clientX - dragStartPos.current.x;
      const deltaY = e.clientY - dragStartPos.current.y;

      moveIcon(icon.id, {
        x: iconStartPos.current.x + deltaX,
        y: iconStartPos.current.y + deltaY,
      });
    };

    const handleMouseUp = () => {
      setDraggingId(null);
      setDragging(false);
      document.removeEventListener('mousemove', handleMouseMove);
      document.removeEventListener('mouseup', handleMouseUp);
    };

    document.addEventListener('mousemove', handleMouseMove);
    document.addEventListener('mouseup', handleMouseUp);
  };

  return (
    <div
      className="desktop absolute inset-0 p-4 grid grid-cols-[repeat(auto-fill,80px)] gap-2 content-start"
      onClick={() => selectIcon('')}
    >
      {icons.map(icon => (
        <div
          key={icon.id}
          className={`desktop-icon flex flex-col items-center gap-1 p-2 rounded cursor-pointer transition-colors ${
            selectedIcon === icon.id ? 'bg-blue-500/30' : 'hover:bg-white/10'
          } ${draggingId === icon.id ? 'opacity-50' : ''}`}
          style={{
            position: 'absolute',
            left: icon.position.x,
            top: icon.position.y,
            width: ICON_SIZE,
          }}
          onMouseDown={(e) => handleIconMouseDown(e, icon)}
          onDoubleClick={icon.onClick}
        >
          <span className="text-4xl">{icon.icon}</span>
          <span className="text-xs text-white text-center truncate w-full">
            {icon.name}
          </span>
        </div>
      ))}
    </div>
  );
};
```

##### 右键菜单实现

```typescript
// 右键菜单组件
import React, { useState, useEffect, useRef } from 'react';

interface MenuItem {
  id: string;
  label: string;
  icon?: string;
  shortcut?: string;
  disabled?: boolean;
  divider?: boolean;
  onClick?: () => void;
  children?: MenuItem[];
}

interface ContextMenuProps {
  items: MenuItem[];
  x: number;
  y: number;
  onClose: () => void;
}

export const ContextMenu: React.FC<ContextMenuProps> = ({ items, x, y, onClose }) => {
  const menuRef = useRef<HTMLDivElement>(null);

  // 菜单位置调整（防止溢出屏幕）
  useEffect(() => {
    if (menuRef.current) {
      const rect = menuRef.current.getBoundingClientRect();
      const viewportWidth = window.innerWidth;
      const viewportHeight = window.innerHeight;

      let adjustedX = x;
      let adjustedY = y;

      if (x + rect.width > viewportWidth) {
        adjustedX = viewportWidth - rect.width - 10;
      }
      if (y + rect.height > viewportHeight) {
        adjustedY = viewportHeight - rect.height - 10;
      }

      menuRef.current.style.left = `${adjustedX}px`;
      menuRef.current.style.top = `${adjustedY}px`;
    }
  }, [x, y]);

  // 点击外部关闭菜单
  useEffect(() => {
    const handleClickOutside = (e: MouseEvent) => {
      if (menuRef.current && !menuRef.current.contains(e.target as Node)) {
        onClose();
      }
    };

    document.addEventListener('mousedown', handleClickOutside);
    return () => document.removeEventListener('mousedown', handleClickOutside);
  }, [onClose]);

  const renderMenuItem = (item: MenuItem, index: number) => {
    if (item.divider) {
      return <div key={index} className="border-t border-gray-600 my-1" />;
    }

    return (
      <button
        key={item.id}
        className={`w-full flex items-center gap-3 px-3 py-2 text-sm text-left hover:bg-blue-600 ${
          item.disabled ? 'opacity-50 cursor-not-allowed' : ''
        }`}
        onClick={() => {
          if (!item.disabled) {
            item.onClick?.();
            onClose();
          }
        }}
      >
        {item.icon && <span>{item.icon}</span>}
        <span className="flex-1">{item.label}</span>
        {item.shortcut && (
          <span className="text-xs text-gray-400">{item.shortcut}</span>
        )}
      </button>
    );
  };

  return (
    <div
      ref={menuRef}
      className="context-menu fixed bg-gray-800 rounded-lg shadow-xl py-1 min-w-[180px] z-[10000]"
      style={{ left: x, top: y }}
    >
      {items.map((item, index) => renderMenuItem(item, index))}
    </div>
  );
};

// 使用示例
export const useContextMenu = () => {
  const [menuState, setMenuState] = useState<{
    visible: boolean;
    x: number;
    y: number;
    items: MenuItem[];
  }>({
    visible: false,
    x: 0,
    y: 0,
    items: [],
  });

  const showMenu = (e: React.MouseEvent, items: MenuItem[]) => {
    e.preventDefault();
    setMenuState({
      visible: true,
      x: e.clientX,
      y: e.clientY,
      items,
    });
  };

  const hideMenu = () => {
    setMenuState(prev => ({ ...prev, visible: false }));
  };

  return { menuState, showMenu, hideMenu };
};
```

##### 壁纸更换功能

```typescript
// 壁纸管理 Hook
import { create } from 'zustand';
import { persist } from 'zustand/middleware';

interface WallpaperState {
  currentWallpaper: string;
  wallpapers: Wallpaper[];

  // 操作
  setWallpaper: (id: string) => void;
  addWallpaper: (wallpaper: Wallpaper) => void;
  removeWallpaper: (id: string) => void;
}

interface Wallpaper {
  id: string;
  name: string;
  url: string;
  thumbnail?: string;
}

const defaultWallpapers: Wallpaper[] = [
  { id: '1', name: '默认蓝', url: '/wallpapers/blue.jpg' },
  { id: '2', name: '星空', url: '/wallpapers/stars.jpg' },
  { id: '3', name: '山脉', url: '/wallpapers/mountain.jpg' },
  { id: '4', name: '城市', url: '/wallpapers/city.jpg' },
  { id: '5', name: '渐变', url: '/wallpapers/gradient.jpg' },
];

const useWallpaperStore = create<WallpaperState>()(
  persist(
    (set) => ({
      currentWallpaper: '/wallpapers/default.jpg',
      wallpapers: defaultWallpapers,

      setWallpaper: (id) => {
        set((state) => {
          const wallpaper = state.wallpapers.find(w => w.id === id);
          if (wallpaper) {
            return { currentWallpaper: wallpaper.url };
          }
          return state;
        });
      },

      addWallpaper: (wallpaper) => {
        set((state) => ({
          wallpapers: [...state.wallpapers, wallpaper],
        }));
      },

      removeWallpaper: (id) => {
        set((state) => ({
          wallpapers: state.wallpapers.filter(w => w.id !== id),
        }));
      },
    }),
    {
      name: 'wallpaper-storage',
    }
  )
);

// 壁纸组件
export const Desktop: React.FC = () => {
  const { currentWallpaper } = useWallpaperStore();

  return (
    <div
      className="desktop absolute inset-0"
      style={{
        backgroundImage: `url(${currentWallpaper})`,
        backgroundSize: 'cover',
        backgroundPosition: 'center',
      }}
    >
      {/* 桌面内容 */}
    </div>
  );
};

// 壁纸选择面板
export const WallpaperPanel: React.FC<{ onClose: () => void }> = ({ onClose }) => {
  const { wallpapers, currentWallpaper, setWallpaper } = useWallpaperStore();

  return (
    <div className="wallpaper-panel bg-gray-800 rounded-lg p-4 w-80">
      <h3 className="text-lg font-bold mb-4">选择壁纸</h3>
      <div className="grid grid-cols-2 gap-3">
        {wallpapers.map(wallpaper => (
          <button
            key={wallpaper.id}
            className={`wallpaper-option rounded-lg overflow-hidden border-2 ${
              currentWallpaper === wallpaper.url ? 'border-blue-500' : 'border-transparent'
            }`}
            onClick={() => {
              setWallpaper(wallpaper.id);
              onClose();
            }}
          >
            <img
              src={wallpaper.thumbnail || wallpaper.url}
              alt={wallpaper.name}
              className="w-full h-24 object-cover"
            />
            <span className="text-xs block p-1">{wallpaper.name}</span>
          </button>
        ))}
      </div>
    </div>
  );
};
```

##### 通知系统实现

```typescript
// 通知系统 Hook + 组件
import React, { createContext, useContext, useState, useCallback } from 'react';
import { create } from 'zustand';

interface Notification {
  id: string;
  type: 'info' | 'success' | 'warning' | 'error';
  title: string;
  message: string;
  duration?: number;
  timestamp: Date;
}

interface NotificationState {
  notifications: Notification[];
  addNotification: (notification: Omit<Notification, 'id' | 'timestamp'>) => void;
  removeNotification: (id: string) => void;
  clearAll: () => void;
}

const useNotificationStore = create<NotificationState>((set) => ({
  notifications: [],

  addNotification: (notification) => {
    const id = `notification-${Date.now()}-${Math.random()}`;
    const newNotification: Notification = {
      ...notification,
      id,
      timestamp: new Date(),
    };

    set((state) => ({
      notifications: [...state.notifications, newNotification],
    }));

    // 自动移除
    const duration = notification.duration ?? 5000;
    if (duration > 0) {
      setTimeout(() => {
        set((state) => ({
          notifications: state.notifications.filter(n => n.id !== id),
        }));
      }, duration);
    }
  },

  removeNotification: (id) => {
    set((state) => ({
      notifications: state.notifications.filter(n => n.id !== id),
    }));
  },

  clearAll: () => {
    set({ notifications: [] });
  },
}));

// 通知组件
export const NotificationContainer: React.FC = () => {
  const { notifications, removeNotification } = useNotificationStore();

  const getTypeStyles = (type: Notification['type']) => {
    const styles = {
      info: 'bg-blue-500',
      success: 'bg-green-500',
      warning: 'bg-yellow-500',
      error: 'bg-red-500',
    };
    return styles[type];
  };

  const getTypeIcon = (type: Notification['type']) => {
    const icons = {
      info: 'ℹ️',
      success: '✓',
      warning: '⚠',
      error: '✕',
    };
    return icons[type];
  };

  return (
    <div className="fixed top-4 right-4 z-[10000] flex flex-col gap-2">
      {notifications.map((notification) => (
        <div
          key={notification.id}
          className={`notification flex items-start gap-3 p-4 rounded-lg shadow-lg text-white min-w-[300px] max-w-[400px] animate-slide-in ${getTypeStyles(notification.type)}`}
        >
          <span className="text-xl">{getTypeIcon(notification.type)}</span>
          <div className="flex-1">
            <h4 className="font-bold">{notification.title}</h4>
            <p className="text-sm opacity-90">{notification.message}</p>
          </div>
          <button
            className="text-white/80 hover:text-white"
            onClick={() => removeNotification(notification.id)}
          >
            ✕
          </button>
        </div>
      ))}
    </div>
  );
};

// 使用 Hook
export const useNotification = () => {
  const { addNotification } = useNotificationStore();

  return {
    info: (title: string, message: string) =>
      addNotification({ type: 'info', title, message }),
    success: (title: string, message: string) =>
      addNotification({ type: 'success', title, message }),
    warning: (title: string, message: string) =>
      addNotification({ type: 'warning', title, message }),
    error: (title: string, message: string) =>
      addNotification({ type: 'error', title, message }),
  };
};
```

##### 窗口动画效果（Framer Motion）

```typescript
// 窗口动画组件
import { motion, AnimatePresence } from 'framer-motion';

// 窗口打开动画
export const windowVariants = {
  hidden: {
    opacity: 0,
    scale: 0.8,
    y: 20,
  },
  visible: {
    opacity: 1,
    scale: 1,
    y: 0,
    transition: {
      type: 'spring',
      stiffness: 300,
      damping: 25,
    },
  },
  exit: {
    opacity: 0,
    scale: 0.8,
    y: 20,
    transition: {
      duration: 0.2,
    },
  },
};

// 最大化动画
export const maximizeVariants = {
  normal: {
    width: 500,
    height: 400,
    borderRadius: 8,
  },
  maximized: {
    width: '100vw',
    height: 'calc(100vh - 48px)', // 减去任务栏高度
    borderRadius: 0,
    transition: {
      type: 'spring',
      stiffness: 200,
      damping: 30,
    },
  },
};

// 使用示例
export const AnimatedWindow: React.FC<{
  isOpen: boolean;
  onClose: () => void;
  isMaximized: boolean;
  onMaximize: () => void;
  children: React.ReactNode;
}> = ({ isOpen, onClose, isMaximized, onMaximize, children }) => {
  return (
    <AnimatePresence>
      {isOpen && (
        <motion.div
          className="window bg-gray-800 rounded-lg overflow-hidden shadow-2xl"
          variants={windowVariants}
          initial="hidden"
          animate="visible"
          exit="exit"
          style={isMaximized ? {
            position: 'fixed',
            top: 0,
            left: 0,
            width: '100vw',
            height: 'calc(100vh - 48px)',
            borderRadius: 0,
          } : undefined}
        >
          {/* 标题栏 */}
          <motion.div className="titlebar flex items-center justify-between px-4 py-2 bg-gray-700">
            <span>窗口标题</span>
            <div className="flex gap-2">
              <button onClick={onMaximize}>□</button>
              <button onClick={onClose}>✕</button>
            </div>
          </motion.div>

          {/* 内容 */}
          <div className="content p-4">
            {children}
          </div>
        </motion.div>
      )}
    </AnimatePresence>
  );
};
```

**面试考察点：**
- Framer Motion 动画配置
- AnimatePresence 条件渲染动画
- Spring 物理动画
- CSS 动画性能优化

### 5.5 学习途径与水平展示

#### 5.5.1 技术学习路径

```
前端学习路线：
┣━━ 入门阶段 (1-3个月)

┃   ┃   ┣━━ 语义化标签

┃   ┗━━ 实战：Todo 列表、博客系统
┣━━ 工程化阶段 (6-9个月)
┃   ┣━━ Webpack/Vite

┃   ┃   ┣━━ 首屏加载优化

┃   ┃   ┣━━ 状态管理架构

┃       ┣━━ Next.js/Nuxt

┗━━ 专家阶段 (1年以上)
    ┣━━ 微前端
    ┃   ┣━━ qiankun
    ┃   ┣━━ Module Federation
    ┃   ┗━━ 沙箱隔离

    ┃   ┣━━ 可视化搭建

    ┗━━ AI/大模型应用
        ┣━━ LLM API 集成

```

#### 5.5.2 技术水平评估标准

```
初级前端 (1-2年):

资深前端/技术专家 (6年+):
┣━━ 技能要求
┃   ┣━━ 技术战略规划
┃   ┣━━ 团队建设

#### 5.5.4 前端技术全景图

```
┏━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━┓   
┃                            前端知识体系                                        ┃
┃  基础层                                                                     ┃   
┃  ┣━━ HTML5 (语义化标签, 表单, API)                                          ┃   
┃  ┃   ┣━━ 语义化标签 (header, nav, article, section, footer)              ┃      
┃  ┃   ┣━━ 表单增强 (input types, validation, formdata)                     ┃     
┃  ┃   ┗━━ API (Canvas, WebGL, WebRTC, Geolocation)                        ┃      
┃  ┣━━ CSS3 (布局, 动画, 响应式)                                             ┃    
┃  ┃   ┣━━ 布局 (Flexbox, Grid, Box Model)                                  ┃     
┃  ┃   ┣━━ 动画 (transition, animation, transform)                          ┃     
┃  ┃   ┣━━ 响应式 (media queries, container queries)                        ┃     
┃  ┃   ┗━━ CSS 预处理器 (Sass, Less, PostCSS)                               ┃     
┃  ┣━━ JavaScript (ES6+, TS, 设计模式)                                       ┃    
┃  ┃   ┣━━ ES6+ (解构, 箭头函数, Promise, async/await, 模块化)              ┃     
┃  ┃   ┣━━ TypeScript (类型系统, 泛型, 工具类型)                             ┃    
┃  ┃   ┗━━ 设计模式 (单例, 工厂, 观察者, 发布订阅)                           ┃    
┃  ┗━━ 计算机网络 (HTTP, WebSocket, 安全)                                     ┃   
┃      ┣━━ HTTP/HTTPS (1.1, 2, 3, 缓存, CORS)                                ┃

#### 5.5.5 框架对比与选型

##### React vs Vue vs Angular 对比

| 对比维度 | React | Vue | Angular |
|---------|-------|-----|---------|
| **学习曲线** | 中等 | 较平缓 | 陡峭 |
| **社区生态** | 非常活跃 | 活跃 | 活跃 |
| **状态管理** | Redux/Zustand/Jotai | Pinia/Vuex | NgRx/Signal |
| **渲染方式** | Virtual DOM | Virtual DOM | 脏检查 |
| **数据绑定** | 单向为主 | 双向(可选) | 双向 |
| **TypeScript** | 推荐支持 | 原生支持 | 原生支持 |
| **打包体积** | 较小 | 最小 | 较大 |
| **灵活性** | 高 | 中 | 低 |
| **适用场景** | 复杂交互/大型应用 | 中小型项目 | 企业级应用 |
| **企业使用** | Meta, Airbnb, Netflix | 阿里巴巴, 字节 | Google, 微软 |

##### 状态管理选型指南

| 场景 | 推荐方案 | 说明 |
|------|----------|------|
| **简单状态** | React Context / Vue provide | 无需额外依赖 |
| **中等复杂度** | Zustand / Pinia | 轻量级 API |
| **复杂企业级** | Redux Toolkit / NgRx | 严格架构 |
| **服务端数据** | React Query / SWR / TanStack Query | 数据同步/缓存 |
| **持久化状态** | zustand/persist | 本地存储 |
| **协作应用** | Yjs + 状态绑定 | CRDT |
| **原子化状态** | Jotai / Recoil | 原子化管理 |
| **全局配置** | React Context + useReducer | 主题/语言 |

##### 构建工具选型

| 场景 | 推荐工具 | 理由 |
|------|----------|------|
| **大型项目** | Webpack 5 | 成熟生态，插件丰富 |
| **中小型项目** | Vite | 开发体验好，HMR 快 |
| **Next.js 项目** | Turbopack | 官方集成，构建快 |
| **库/组件** | Rollup | Tree Shaking 好 |
| **极致速度** | esbuild | Go 实现，极速 |
| **现代框架** | Parcel | 零配置 |

##### 组件库选型

| 类型 | 推荐 | 特点 |
|------|------|------|
| **React 企业级** | Ant Design | 功能全面，文档好 |
| **React 轻量级** | Chakra UI / Headless UI | 可定制，灵活 |
| **Vue 企业级** | Element Plus | 饿了么出品 |
| **Vue 轻量级** | Naive UI | 组件丰富，TypeScript |
| **移动端** | Vant (有赞) | 移动端优先 |
| **无样式** | Radix UI / Headless UI | 可访问性 |

##### 编辑器技术选型

| 场景 | 推荐方案 | 关键特性 |
|------|----------|----------|
| **富文本编辑** | TipTap | ProseMirror, Yjs 支持 |
| **代码编辑** | Monaco Editor | VS Code 同款 |
| **Markdown** | Milkdown / ByteMD | 所见即所得 |
| **表格编辑** | Handsontable | Excel 体验 |
| **块编辑器** | Editor.js | 块式结构 |

##### 实时协作技术选型

| 需求 | 推荐方案 | 备注 |
|------|----------|------|
| **文本协作** | Yjs | CRDT, 性能好 |
| **结构化数据** | Automerge | JSON-like |
| **实时同步** | Socket.io / WebSocket | 基础实时 |
| **视频会议** | LiveKit / Agora | WebRTC |
| **状态同步** | CRDT | 离线优先 |

---

## 七、常见场景题

### 6.1 无限滚动实现

```javascript
// 无限滚动组件
function InfiniteScroll({
  loadMore,
  hasMore,
  loader = <div>Loading...</div>,
  threshold = 200
}) {
  const observerRef = useRef(null);
  const loadingRef = useRef(false);

  const lastElementRef = useCallback(node => {
    if (loadingRef.current) return;

    if (observerRef.current) observerRef.current.disconnect();

    observerRef.current = new IntersectionObserver(entries => {
      if (entries[0].isIntersecting && hasMore && !loadingRef.current) {
        loadingRef.current = true;
        Promise.resolve(loadMore()).finally(() => {
          loadingRef.current = false;
        });
      }
    }, { rootMargin: `${threshold}px` });

    if (node) observerRef.current.observe(node);
  }, [loadMore, hasMore, threshold]);

  return (
    <div>
      {children}
      {hasMore && <div ref={lastElementRef}>{loader}</div>}
    </div>
  );
}

// 使用示例
function UserList() {
  const [users, setUsers] = useState([]);
  const [page, setPage] = useState(1);
  const [hasMore, setHasMore] = useState(true);

  const loadMore = async () => {
    const newUsers = await fetchUsers(page);
    if (newUsers.length === 0) {
      setHasMore(false);
    } else {
      setUsers(prev => [...prev, ...newUsers]);
      setPage(prev => prev + 1);
    }
  };

  return (
    <InfiniteScroll loadMore={loadMore} hasMore={hasMore}>
      {users.map(user => (
        <UserCard key={user.id} user={user} />
      ))}
    </InfiniteScroll>
  );
}
```

### 6.2 大文件上传

```javascript
// 分片上传实现
class ChunkUploader {
  constructor(file, options = {}) {
    this.file = file;
    this.chunkSize = options.chunkSize || 2 * 1024 * 1024; // 2MB
    this.concurrent = options.concurrent || 3;
    this.onProgress = options.onProgress || (() => {});
  }

  async upload() {
    const chunks = this.createChunks();
    const uploaded = [];

    // 上传每个分片
    for (let i = 0; i < chunks.length; i += this.concurrent) {
      const batch = chunks.slice(i, i + this.concurrent);
      const results = await Promise.all(
        batch.map(chunk => this.uploadChunk(chunk))
      );
      uploaded.push(...results);

      const progress = (uploaded.length / chunks.length) * 100;
      this.onProgress(progress);
    }

    // 合并分片
    await this.mergeChunks(uploaded);

    return uploaded;
  }

  createChunks() {
    const chunks = [];
    let start = 0;

    while (start < this.file.size) {
      const end = Math.min(start + this.chunkSize, this.file.size);
      chunks.push({
        start,
        end,
        blob: this.file.slice(start, end),
        hash: this.calculateHash(start, end)
      });
      start = end;
    }

    return chunks;
  }

  async uploadChunk(chunk) {
    const formData = new FormData();
    formData.append('chunk', chunk.blob);
    formData.append('hash', chunk.hash);
    formData.append('index', chunk.start / this.chunkSize);

    await fetch('/api/upload/chunk', {
      method: 'POST',
      body: formData
    });

    return chunk.hash;
  }

  calculateHash(start, end) {
    // 简化版：使用 slice 位置作为 hash
    return `${start}-${end}`;
  }

  async mergeChunks(hashes) {
    await fetch('/api/upload/merge', {
      method: 'POST',
      headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
      body: JSON.stringify({
        fileName: this.file.name,
        hashes
      })
    });
  }
}

// 使用示例
function FileUploader() {
  const [progress, setProgress] = useState(0);

  const handleFileChange = async (e) => {
    const file = e.target.files[0];
    if (!file) return;

    const uploader = new ChunkUploader(file, {
      chunkSize: 1024 * 1024, // 1MB
      concurrent: 2,
      onProgress: setProgress
    });

    await uploader.upload();
    console.log('Upload complete');
  };

  return (
    <div>
      <input type="file" onChange={handleFileChange} />
      <progress value={progress} max="100" />
    </div>
  );
}
```

### 6.3 实时聊天系统

```javascript
// 实时聊天系统
function useChat(roomId) {
  const [messages, setMessages] = useState([]);
  const [connectionStatus, setConnectionStatus] = useState('disconnected');
  const wsRef = useRef(null);
  const reconnectTimerRef = useRef(null);

  // 连接 WebSocket
  const connect = useCallback(() => {
    wsRef.current = new WebSocket(`wss://chat.example.com/room/${roomId}`);

    wsRef.current.onopen = () => {
      setConnectionStatus('connected');
      clearTimeout(reconnectTimerRef.current);
    };

    wsRef.current.onmessage = (event) => {
      const message = JSON.parse(event.data);
      setMessages(prev => [...prev, message]);
    };

    wsRef.current.onclose = () => {
      setConnectionStatus('disconnected');
      // 自动重连
      reconnectTimerRef.current = setTimeout(connect, 3000);
    };

    wsRef.current.onerror = (error) => {
      console.error('WebSocket error:', error);
    };
  }, [roomId]);

  // 发送消息
  const sendMessage = useCallback((content) => {
    if (wsRef.current?.readyState === WebSocket.OPEN) {
      wsRef.current.send(JSON.stringify({
        type: 'message',
        content,
        timestamp: Date.now()
      }));
    }
  }, []);

  // 断开连接
  const disconnect = useCallback(() => {
    clearTimeout(reconnectTimerRef.current);
    wsRef.current?.close();
  }, []);

  useEffect(() => {
    connect();
    return () => disconnect();
  }, [connect, disconnect]);

  return { messages, sendMessage, connectionStatus };
}

// 聊天组件
function ChatRoom({ roomId }) {
  const { messages, sendMessage, connectionStatus } = useChat(roomId);
  const [input, setInput] = useState('');
  const messagesEndRef = useRef(null);

  const handleSend = () => {
    if (input.trim()) {
      sendMessage(input);
      setInput('');
    }
  };

  useEffect(() => {
    messagesEndRef.current?.scrollIntoView({ behavior: 'smooth' });
  }, [messages]);

  return (
    <div className="chat-room">
      <div className="status">
        Status: {connectionStatus}
      </div>
      <div className="messages">
        {messages.map((msg, i) => (
          <div key={i} className="message">
            {msg.content}
          </div>
        ))}
        <div ref={messagesEndRef} />
      </div>
      <div className="input-area">
        <input
          value={input}
          onChange={(e) => setInput(e.target.value)}
          onKeyPress={(e) => e.key === 'Enter' && handleSend()}
        />
        <button onClick={handleSend}>Send</button>
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}
```

### 6.4 搜索建议功能

```javascript
// 防抖搜索 Hook
function useSearchSuggestions(searchFn, debounceMs = 300) {
  const [query, setQuery] = useState('');
  const [suggestions, setSuggestions] = useState([]);
  const [loading, setLoading] = useState(false);
  const debouncedSearch = useMemo(
    () => debounce(async (searchQuery) => {
      if (!searchQuery.trim()) {
        setSuggestions([]);
        return;
      }

      setLoading(true);
      try {
        const results = await searchFn(searchQuery);
        setSuggestions(results);
      } catch (error) {
        console.error('Search error:', error);
      } finally {
        setLoading(false);
      }
    }, debounceMs),
    [searchFn, debounceMs]
  );

  useEffect(() => {
    debouncedSearch(query);
  }, [query, debouncedSearch]);

  const clearSuggestions = useCallback(() => {
    setSuggestions([]);
    setQuery('');
  }, []);

  return { query, setQuery, suggestions, loading, clearSuggestions };
}

// 搜索建议组件
function SearchInput() {
  const { query, setQuery, suggestions, loading } = useSearchSuggestions(
    async (searchQuery) => {
      // 模拟 API 调用
      const response = await fetch(`/api/search?q=${searchQuery}`);
      return response.json();
    }
  );

  return (
    <div className="search-container">
      <input
        value={query}
        onChange={(e) => setQuery(e.target.value)}
        placeholder="Search..."
      />
      {loading && <span className="loading">Loading...</span>}
      {suggestions.length > 0 && (
        <ul className="suggestions">
          {suggestions.map((item) => (
            <li
              key={item.id}
              onClick={() => {
                setQuery(item.text);
                setSuggestions([]);
              }}
            >
              {highlightMatch(item.text, query)}
            </li>
          ))}
        </ul>
      )}
    </div>
  );
}

// 高亮匹配文本
function highlightMatch(text, query) {
  if (!query) return text;

  const regex = new RegExp(`(${query})`, 'gi');
  const parts = text.split(regex);

  return parts.map((part, i) =>
    regex.test(part) ? <mark key={i}>{part}</mark> : part
  );
}
```

### 6.5 级联选择器（省市区选择）

```javascript
// 省市区数据（实际项目中通常从接口获取）
const regionData = [
  {
    value: '110000',
    label: '北京市',
    children: [
      {
        value: '110100',
        label: '市辖区',
        children: [
          { value: '110101', label: '东城区' },
          { value: '110102', label: '西城区' },
          { value: '110105', label: '朝阳区' },
          { value: '110106', label: '丰台区' },
          { value: '110107', label: '石景山区' },
          { value: '110108', label: '海淀区' }
        ]
      }
    ]
  },
  {
    value: '310000',
    label: '上海市',
    children: [
      {
        value: '310100',
        label: '市辖区',
        children: [
          { value: '310101', label: '黄浦区' },
          { value: '310104', label: '徐汇区' },
          { value: '310105', label: '长宁区' },
          { value: '310106', label: '静安区' },
          { value: '310107', label: '普陀区' },
          { value: '310109', label: '虹口区' }
        ]
      }
    ]
  }
];

// 级联选择器组件
function CascaderSelect({ value, onChange, options = regionData }) {
  const [selectedOptions, setSelectedOptions] = useState([]);

  // 加载子级数据（实际项目中可能需要异步加载）
  const loadData = useCallback((selectedOptions) => {
    const targetValue = selectedOptions[selectedOptions.length - 1].value;
    // 模拟异步加载
    return new Promise((resolve) => {
      setTimeout(() => {
        // 实际项目中这里从接口获取数据
        resolve();
      }, 300);
    });
  }, []);

  const handleChange = (value, selectedOptions) => {
    setSelectedOptions(selectedOptions);
    onChange?.(value);
  };

  return (
    <Cascader
      options={options}
      value={value}
      onChange={handleChange}
      loadData={loadData}
      placeholder="请选择省市区"
      changeOnSelect
    />
  );
}

// 使用示例
function AddressForm() {
  const [address, setAddress] = useState([]);

  const handleSubmit = () => {
    const [province, city, district] = address;
    console.log('选择的地址:', {
      province: province,
      city: city,
      district: district
    });
  };

  return (
    <form>
      <CascaderSelect
        value={address}
        onChange={setAddress}
      />
      <button type="button" onClick={handleSubmit}>提交</button>
    </form>
  );
}

// 手写级联选择器（简化版）
function SimpleCascader({ options, value, onChange }) {
  const [currentLevel, setCurrentLevel] = useState(0);
  const [path, setPath] = useState([]);

  const currentOptions = path.length === 0
    ? options
    : path[path.length - 1].children || [];

  const handleSelect = (option) => {
    const newPath = [...path, option];
    setPath(newPath);
    setCurrentLevel(newPath.length);

    const values = newPath.map(p => p.value);
    onChange?.(values);

    // 如果有子级，继续展开；否则关闭
    if (option.children && option.children.length > 0) {
      // 等待用户选择
    } else {
      // 已选中最后一级
    }
  };

  const handleBack = (index) => {
    const newPath = path.slice(0, index + 1);
    setPath(newPath);
    setCurrentLevel(newPath.length);
  };

  return (
    <div className="cascader">
      {/* 已选路径 */}
      {path.length > 0 && (
        <div className="cascader-path">
          {path.map((item, index) => (
            <span key={index}>
              <span onClick={() => handleBack(index)}>{item.label}</span>
              {index < path.length - 1 && ' / '}
            </span>
          ))}
        </div>
      )}

      {/* 选项列表 */}
      <div className="cascader-panel">
        {currentOptions.map(option => (
          <div
            key={option.value}
            className="cascader-option"
            onClick={() => handleSelect(option)}
          >
            {option.label}
            {option.children && option.children.length > 0 && ' >'}
          </div>
        ))}
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}
```

### 6.6 日期范围选择器

```javascript
// 日期范围选择器
function DateRangePicker({ value, onChange, format = 'YYYY-MM-DD' }) {
  const [startDate, setStartDate] = useState(value?.[0] || null);
  const [endDate, setEndDate] = useState(value?.[1] || null);
  const [isOpen, setIsOpen] = useState(false);
  const [currentMonth, setCurrentMonth] = useState(new Date());

  // 生成日历数据
  const generateCalendarDays = (date) => {
    const year = date.getFullYear();
    const month = date.getMonth();
    const firstDay = new Date(year, month, 1);
    const lastDay = new Date(year, month + 1, 0);
    const startPadding = firstDay.getDay();
    const days = [];

    // 填充上个月的天数
    for (let i = startPadding - 1; i >= 0; i--) {
      const d = new Date(year, month, -i);
      days.push({ date: d, isCurrentMonth: false });
    }

    // 当月天数
    for (let i = 1; i <= lastDay.getDate(); i++) {
      days.push({ date: new Date(year, month, i), isCurrentMonth: true });
    }

    // 填充下个月的天数
    const remaining = 42 - days.length;
    for (let i = 1; i <= remaining; i++) {
      days.push({ date: new Date(year, month + 1, i), isCurrentMonth: false });
    }

    return days;
  };

  const calendarDays = generateCalendarDays(currentMonth);

  const isInRange = (date) => {
    if (!startDate || !endDate) return false;
    return date >= startDate && date <= endDate;
  };

  const isStartOrEnd = (date) => {
    if (!startDate || !endDate) return false;
    const dateStr = date.toDateString();
    return dateStr === startDate.toDateString() ||
           dateStr === endDate.toDateString();
  };

  const handleDateClick = (date) => {
    if (!startDate || (startDate && endDate)) {
      // 重新开始选择
      setStartDate(date);
      setEndDate(null);
    } else if (date < startDate) {
      // 开始日期大于结束日期，重新选择
      setStartDate(date);
    } else {
      // 选择结束日期
      setEndDate(date);
      onChange?.([startDate, date]);
      setIsOpen(false);
    }
  };

  const formatDate = (date, fmt) => {
    if (!date) return '';
    const d = new Date(date);
    const o = {
      'YYYY': d.getFullYear(),
      'MM': String(d.getMonth() + 1).padStart(2, '0'),
      'DD': String(d.getDate()).padStart(2, '0')
    };
    return fmt.replace(/YYYY|MM|DD/g, matched => o[matched]);
  };

  const goToPrevMonth = () => {
    setCurrentMonth(new Date(currentMonth.getFullYear(), currentMonth.getMonth() - 1));
  };

  const goToNextMonth = () => {
    setCurrentMonth(new Date(currentMonth.getFullYear(), currentMonth.getMonth() + 1));
  };

  return (
    <div className="date-range-picker">
      <input
        readOnly
        value={`${formatDate(startDate, format)} - ${formatDate(endDate, format)}`}
        onClick={() => setIsOpen(!isOpen)}
        placeholder="选择日期范围"
      />

      {isOpen && (
        <div className="date-picker-dropdown">
          <div className="calendar-header">
            <button onClick={goToPrevMonth}>&lt;</button>
            <span>
              {currentMonth.getFullYear()}年{currentMonth.getMonth() + 1}月
            </span>
            <button onClick={goToNextMonth}>&gt;</button>
          </div>

          <div className="calendar-weekdays">
            {['日', '一', '二', '三', '四', '五', '六'].map(day => (
              <div key={day}>{day}</div>
            ))}
          </div>

          <div className="calendar-days">
            {calendarDays.map(({ date, isCurrentMonth }, index) => {
              const inRange = isInRange(date);
              const isStartOrEndDate = isStartOrEnd(date);
              const isToday = date.toDateString() === new Date().toDateString();

              return (
                <div
                  key={index}
                  className={`calendar-day ${!isCurrentMonth ? 'other-month' : ''} ${
                    inRange ? 'in-range' : ''
                  } ${isStartOrEndDate ? 'selected' : ''} ${isToday ? 'today' : ''}`}
                  onClick={() => handleDateClick(date)}
                >
                  {date.getDate()}
                </div>
              );
            })}
          </div>
        </div>
      )}
    </div>
  );
}

// 使用快捷选项
function DateRangePickerWithShortcuts({ value, onChange }) {
  const [selectedRange, setSelectedRange] = useState(value);

  const shortcuts = [
    { label: '今天', value: [new Date(), new Date()] },
    { label: '昨天', value: [new Date(Date.now() - 86400000), new Date(Date.now() - 86400000)] },
    { label: '最近7天', value: [new Date(Date.now() - 7 * 86400000), new Date()] },
    { label: '最近30天', value: [new Date(Date.now() - 30 * 86400000), new Date()] },
    { label: '本月', value: [new Date(new Date().getFullYear(), new Date().getMonth(), 1), new Date()] },
    { label: '本年', value: [new Date(new Date().getFullYear(), 0, 1), new Date()] }
  ];

  const handleShortcutClick = (shortcut) => {
    setSelectedRange(shortcut.value);
    onChange?.(shortcut.value);
  };

  return (
    <div>
      <div className="shortcuts">
        {shortcuts.map(shortcut => (
          <button key={shortcut.label} onClick={() => handleShortcutClick(shortcut)}>
            {shortcut.label}
          </button>
        ))}
      </div>
      <DateRangePicker value={selectedRange} onChange={setSelectedRange} />
    </div>
  );
}
```

### 6.7 图片上传（单图/多图/拖拽上传）

```javascript
// 单图上传组件
function SingleImageUploader({ value, onChange, maxSize = 5 * 1024 * 1024 }) {
  const [preview, setPreview] = useState(value);
  const [loading, setLoading] = useState(false);
  const [error, setError] = useState(null);
  const inputRef = useRef(null);

  const handleFileChange = async (e) => {
    const file = e.target.files?.[0];
    if (!file) return;

    // 验证文件大小
    if (file.size > maxSize) {
      setError(`文件大小不能超过 ${maxSize / 1024 / 1024}MB`);
      return;
    }

    // 验证文件类型
    if (!file.type.startsWith('image/')) {
      setError('请选择图片文件');
      return;
    }

    setError(null);
    setLoading(true);

    try {
      // 生成预览
      const previewUrl = await generatePreview(file);
      setPreview(previewUrl);

      // 上传到服务器
      const url = await uploadFile(file);
      onChange?.(url);
    } catch (err) {
      setError('上传失败');
    } finally {
      setLoading(false);
    }
  };

  const generatePreview = (file) => {
    return new Promise((resolve) => {
      const reader = new FileReader();
      reader.onload = (e) => resolve(e.target.result);
      reader.readAsDataURL(file);
    });
  };

  const uploadFile = async (file) => {
    const formData = new FormData();
    formData.append('file', file);

    const response = await fetch('/api/upload', {
      method: 'POST',
      body: formData
    });

    const data = await response.json();
    return data.url;
  };

  const handleRemove = () => {
    setPreview(null);
    onChange?.(null);
    if (inputRef.current) {
      inputRef.current.value = '';
    }
  };

  return (
    <div className="single-uploader">
      {preview ? (
        <div className="preview">
          <img src={preview} alt="预览" />
          <div className="actions">
            <button onClick={() => inputRef.current?.click()}>替换</button>
            <button onClick={handleRemove}>删除</button>
          </div>
        </div>
      ) : (
        <div
          className="upload-placeholder"
          onClick={() => inputRef.current?.click()}
        >
          {loading ? '上传中...' : '+ 添加图片'}
        </div>
      )}
      <input
        ref={inputRef}
        type="file"
        accept="image/*"
        onChange={handleFileChange}
        style={{ display: 'none' }}
      />
      {error && <div className="error">{error}</div>}
    </div>
  );
}

// 多图上传组件
function MultipleImageUploader({ value = [], onChange, maxCount = 9 }) {
  const [fileList, setFileList] = useState([]);

  // 初始化已有图片
  useEffect(() => {
    setFileList(value.map((url, index) => ({
      uid: `exist-${index}`,
      url,
      status: 'done'
    })));
  }, [value]);

  const handleFileChange = async (e) => {
    const files = Array.from(e.target.files);

    if (fileList.length + files.length > maxCount) {
      alert(`最多上传 ${maxCount} 张图片`);
      return;
    }

    const newFileList = [];

    for (const file of files) {
      const preview = await generatePreview(file);
      newFileList.push({
        uid: `new-${Date.now()}-${Math.random()}`,
        file,
        url: preview,
        status: 'uploading'
      });
    }

    setFileList(prev => [...prev, ...newFileList]);

    // 依次上传
    for (const item of newFileList) {
      try {
        const uploadedUrl = await uploadFile(item.file);
        setFileList(prev => prev.map(f =>
          f.uid === item.uid
            ? { ...f, url: uploadedUrl, status: 'done' }
            : f
        ));
      } catch (err) {
        setFileList(prev => prev.map(f =>
          f.uid === item.uid
            ? { ...f, status: 'error', error: '上传失败' }
            : f
        ));
      }
    }
  };

  const generatePreview = (file) => {
    return new Promise((resolve) => {
      const reader = new FileReader();
      reader.onload = (e) => resolve(e.target.result);
      reader.readAsDataURL(file);
    });
  };

  const uploadFile = async (file) => {
    const formData = new FormData();
    formData.append('files', file);

    const response = await fetch('/api/upload/multiple', {
      method: 'POST',
      body: formData
    });

    const data = await response.json();
    return data.url;
  };

  const handleRemove = (uid) => {
    const newFileList = fileList.filter(f => f.uid !== uid);
    setFileList(newFileList);
    onChange?.(newFileList.filter(f => f.status === 'done').map(f => f.url));
  };

  const handleReorder = (dragIndex, dropIndex) => {
    const newList = [...fileList];
    const [draggedItem] = newList.splice(dragIndex, 1);
    newList.splice(dropIndex, 0, draggedItem);
    setFileList(newList);
    onChange?.(newList.filter(f => f.status === 'done').map(f => f.url));
  };

  return (
    <div className="multiple-uploader">
      <div className="file-list">
        {fileList.map((item, index) => (
          <div key={item.uid} className="file-item">
            <img src={item.url} alt="" />
            {item.status === 'uploading' && <div className="uploading">上传中...</div>}
            {item.status === 'error' && <div className="error">{item.error}</div>}
            {item.status === 'done' && (
              <>
                <button className="remove" onClick={() => handleRemove(item.uid)}>x</button>
                <div className="drag-handle">::</div>
              </>
            )}
          </div>
        ))}
        {fileList.length < maxCount && (
          <div className="upload-placeholder" onClick={() => document.getElementById('multi-file-input').click()}>
            + 添加
          </div>
        )}
      </div>
      <input
        id="multi-file-input"
        type="file"
        accept="image/*"
        multiple
        onChange={handleFileChange}
        style={{ display: 'none' }}
      />
    </div>
  );
}

// 拖拽上传组件
function DragDropUploader({ onChange }) {
  const [isDragging, setIsDragging] = useState(false);
  const [uploadProgress, setUploadProgress] = useState({});

  const handleDragEnter = (e) => {
    e.preventDefault();
    e.stopPropagation();
    setIsDragging(true);
  };

  const handleDragLeave = (e) => {
    e.preventDefault();
    e.stopPropagation();
    setIsDragging(false);
  };

  const handleDragOver = (e) => {
    e.preventDefault();
    e.stopPropagation();
  };

  const handleDrop = async (e) => {
    e.preventDefault();
    e.stopPropagation();
    setIsDragging(false);

    const files = Array.from(e.dataTransfer.files);
    await handleUpload(files);
  };

  const handleFileInput = async (e) => {
    const files = Array.from(e.target.files);
    await handleUpload(files);
  };

  const handleUpload = async (files) => {
    for (const file of files) {
      if (!file.type.startsWith('image/')) {
        alert('请上传图片文件');
        continue;
      }

      const fileId = `file-${Date.now()}-${Math.random()}`;
      setUploadProgress(prev => ({ ...prev, [fileId]: 0 }));

      await uploadWithProgress(file, (progress) => {
        setUploadProgress(prev => ({ ...prev, [fileId]: progress }));
      });

      setUploadProgress(prev => {
        const newProgress = { ...prev };
        delete newProgress[fileId];
        return newProgress;
      });
    }
  };

  const uploadWithProgress = (file, onProgress) => {
    return new Promise((resolve, reject) => {
      const xhr = new XMLHttpRequest();
      const formData = new FormData();
      formData.append('file', file);

      xhr.upload.onprogress = (e) => {
        if (e.lengthComputable) {
          const progress = Math.round((e.loaded / e.total) * 100);
          onProgress(progress);
        }
      };

      xhr.onload = () => {
        if (xhr.status >= 200 && xhr.status < 300) {
          const response = JSON.parse(xhr.responseText);
          onChange?.(response.url);
          resolve(response.url);
        } else {
          reject(new Error('Upload failed'));
        }
      };

      xhr.onerror = () => reject(new Error('Upload failed'));
      xhr.open('POST', '/api/upload');
      xhr.send(formData);
    });
  };

  return (
    <div
      className={`drag-drop-uploader ${isDragging ? 'dragging' : ''}`}
      onDragEnter={handleDragEnter}
      onDragLeave={handleDragLeave}
      onDragOver={handleDragOver}
      onDrop={handleDrop}
    >
      <div className="upload-content">
        <div className="icon">📁</div>
        <div className="text">拖拽图片到此处上传</div>
        <div className="or">或</div>
        <button onClick={() => document.getElementById('drag-file-input').click()}>
          选择文件
        </button>
      </div>
      <input
        id="drag-file-input"
        type="file"
        accept="image/*"
        multiple
        onChange={handleFileInput}
        style={{ display: 'none' }}
      />
      {Object.keys(uploadProgress).length > 0 && (
        <div className="progress-list">
          {Object.entries(uploadProgress).map(([fileId, progress]) => (
            <div key={fileId} className="progress-item">
              <progress value={progress} max="100" />
              <span>{progress}%</span>
            </div>
          ))}
        </div>
      )}
    </div>
  );
}
```

**面试考察点：**
- 文件上传的基本原理
- FormData 的使用
- XMLHttpRequest 的进度事件
- 图片预览的实现
- 拖拽 API 的使用

**常见追问：**
- 如何实现秒传（根据 MD5）？
- 如何处理上传失败重试？
- 如何限制并发上传数量？
